       ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Vital statistics related to the population are:\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-58">\n        <a </td>\n        <td style="text-align:right;">\n         616.3\n        </td>\n        <td style="text-align:right;">\n         49000\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-cia_4-1">\n          <a href="#cite_note-cia-4">\n           [3]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Language">\n        Language\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Turks_and_Caicos_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Language">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       The official language of the islands is English and the population also speaks\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Turks_and_Caicos_Islands_Creole" title="Turks and Caicos Islands Creole">\n        Turks and Caicos Islands Creole\n       </a>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-62">\n        <a href="#cite_note-62">\n         [59]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       which is similar to\n       <a href="/wiki/Bahamian_Creole" title="Bahamian Creole">\n        Bahamian Creole\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-63">\n        <a href="#cite_note-63">\n         [60]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Due to its close proximity to\n       <a href="/wiki/Cuba" title="Cuba">\n        Cuba\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Hispaniola" title="Hispaniola">\n        Hispaniola\n       </a>\n       , large\n       <a href="/wiki/Haitian_Creole" title="Haitian Creole">\n        Haitian Creole\n       </a>\n       and Spanish-speaking communities have developed in the territory due to immigration, both legal and illegal, from Creole-speaking\n       <a href="/wiki/Haiti" title="Haiti">\n        Haiti\n       </a>\n       and from Spanish-speaking Cuba and\n       <a href="/wiki/Dominican_Republic" title="Dominican Republic">\n        Dominican Republic\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-64">\n        <a href="#cite_note-64">\n         [61]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Religion">\n        Religion\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Turks_and_Caicos_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Religion">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/Religion_in_the_Turks_and_Caicos_Islands" title="Religion in the Turks and Caicos Islands">\n        Religion in the Turks and Caicos Islands\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       72.8% of the population of Turks and Caicos are\n       <a href="/wiki/Christian" title="Christian">\n        Christian\n       </a>\n       (\n       <a href="/wiki/Baptists" title="Baptists">\n        Baptists\n       </a>\n       35.8%,\n       <a href="/wiki/Church_of_God_(Cleveland,_Tennessee)" title="Church of God (Cleveland, Tennessee)">\n        Church of God\n       </a>\n       11.7%,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Roman_Catholics" title="Roman Catholics">\n        Roman Catholics\n       </a>\n       11.4%,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Anglicans" title="Anglicans">\n        Anglicans\n       </a>\n       10%,\n       <a href="/wiki/Methodism" title="Methodism">\n        Methodists\n       </a>\n       9.3%,\n       <a href="/wiki/Seventh-day_Adventist_Church" title="Seventh-day Adventist Church">\n        Seventh-day Adventists\n       </a>\n       6%,\n       <a href="/wiki/Jehovah%27s_Witnesses" title="Jehovah\'s Witnesses">\n        Jehovah\'s Witnesses\n       </a>\n       1.8% and Others 14%).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CIAPAPUANEWGUINEA_57-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-CIAPAPUANEWGUINEA-57">\n         [55]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Catholics are served by the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Mission_Sui_Iuris_of_Turks_and_Caicos" title="Roman Catholic Mission Sui Iuris of Turks and Caicos">\n        Mission "Sui Iuris" for Turks and Caicos\n       </a>\n       , which was erected in 1984 with territory taken from the then\n       <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Archdiocese_of_Nassau" title="Roman Catholic Archdiocese of Nassau">\n        Diocese of Nassau\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Culture">\n        Culture\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Turks_and_Caicos_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Culture">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       See also:\n       <a href="/wiki/Music_of_the_Turks_and_Caicos_Islands" title="Music of the Turks and Caicos Islands">\n        Music of the Turks and Caicos Islands\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Turks_%26_Caicos_National_Museum.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2180" data-file-width="2907" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3a/Turks_%26_Caicos_National_Museum.jpg/220px-Turks_%26_Caicos_National_Museum.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3a/Turks_%26_Caicos_National_Museum.jpg/330px-Turks_%26_Caicos_National_Museum.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3a/Turks_%26_Caicos_National_Museum.jpg/440px-Turks_%26_Caicos_National_Museum.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Turks_%26_Caicos_National_Museum.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Turks and Caicos National Museum on Grand Turk\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The Turks and Caicos Islands are most well known for\n       <a href="/wiki/Ripsaw_music" title="Ripsaw music">\n        ripsaw music\n       </a>\n       . The islands are known for their annual Music and Cultural Festival showcasing many local talents and other dynamic performances by many music celebrities from around the Caribbean and United States.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Women continue traditional crafts of using straw to make baskets and hats on the larger Caicos islands. It is possible that this continued tradition is related to the liberated Africans who joined the population directly from Africa in the 1830s and 1841 from shipwrecked slavers; they brought cultural craft skills with them.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-sadler_23-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-sadler-23">\n         [21]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The island\'s most popular sports are fishing, sailing,\n       <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">\n        football\n       </a>\n       (soccer) and\n       <a href="/wiki/Cricket" title="Cricket">\n        cricket\n       </a>\n       (which is the national sport).\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Turks and Caicos cuisine is based primarily around seafood, especially\n       <a href="/wiki/Conch" title="Conch">\n        conch\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-65">\n        <a href="#cite_note-65">\n         [62]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Two common dishes, whilst not traditionally \'local\', are conch fritters and conch salad.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-66">\n        <a href="#cite_note-66">\n         [63]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Citizenship">\n        Citizenship\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Turks_and_Caicos_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Citizenship">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       See also:\n       <a href="/wiki/British_Overseas_Territories_citizen#Access_to_British_citizenship" title="British Overseas Territories citizen">\n        British Overseas Territories citizen \xc2\xa7\xc2\xa0Access to British citizenship\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Because the Turks and Caicos is a\n       <a href="/wiki/British_Overseas_Territories" title="British Overseas Territories">\n        British Overseas Territory\n       </a>\n       and not an independent country, they, at one time, could not confer citizenship. Instead, people with close ties to Britain\'s Overseas Territories all held the same nationality:\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/British_Overseas_Territories_Citizen" title="British Overseas Territories Citizen">\n        British Overseas Territories Citizen\n       </a>\n       (BOTC) as defined by the\n       <a href="/wiki/British_Nationality_Act_1981" title="British Nationality Act 1981">\n        British Nationality Act 1981\n       </a>\n       and subsequent amendments. BOTC, however, does not confer any right to live in any British Overseas Territory, including the territory from which it is derived. Instead, the rights normally associated with citizenship derive from what is called\n       <a href="/wiki/Belonger_status" title="Belonger status">\n        Belonger status\n       </a>\n       and island natives or descendants from natives are said to be\n       <a href="/wiki/Belonger_status#Belonger_status_in_Turks_and_Caicos" title="Belonger status">\n        Belongers\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In 2002, the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/British_Overseas_Territories_Act" title="British Overseas Territories Act">\n        British Overseas Territories Act\n       </a>\n       restored full British citizenship status to all citizens of British Overseas Territories, including the Turks and Caicos.\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Education_system">\n        Education system\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Turks_and_Caicos_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Education system">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <p>\n       Public Education is supported by taxation, and is mandatory for children aged five to sixteen. Primary education lasts for six years and secondary education lasts for five years. In the 1990s, the island nation launched the Primary In-Service Teacher Education Project (PINSTEP) in an effort to increase the skills of its primary school teachers, nearly one-quarter of whom were unqualified. Turks and Caicos also worked to refurbish its primary schools, reduce textbook costs, and increase equipment and supplies given to schools. For example, in September 1993, each primary school was given enough books to allow teachers to establish in-class libraries.\n       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">\n        [\n        <i>\n         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">\n          <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (April 2010)">\n           citation needed\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </i>\n        ]\n       </sup>\n       In 2001, the student\xe2\x80\x93teacher ratio at the primary level was roughly 15:1.\n       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">\n        [\n        <i>\n         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">\n          <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (April 2010)">\n           citation needed\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </i>\n        ]\n       </sup>\n       The Turks and Caicos Islands Community College offers free higher education to students who have successfully completed their secondary education. The community college also oversees an adult literacy program. The Ministry of Health, Education, Youth, Sports, and Women\'s Affairs oversees education in Turks and Caicos. Once a student completes their education at Turks and Caicos Islands Community College, they are allowed to further their education at a university in the United States, Canada, or the United Kingdom for free. They have to commit to working in The Turks and Caicos Islands for four years to receive this additional education.\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Health_system">\n        Health system\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Turks_and_Caicos_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Health system">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <p>\n       The Turks and Caicos established a National Health System in 2010. Residents contribute to a National Health Insurance Plan through salary deduction and nominal user fees. Majority of care is provided by the private-public-partnership hospitals in Providenciales and Grand Turk. In addition there are a number of government clinics and private clinics. The hospital opened in 2010 is administered by\n       <a href="/wiki/Interhealth_Canada" title="Interhealth Canada">\n        Interhealth Canada\n       </a>\n       and has been accredited by Accreditation Canada in 2012 and 2015.\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Economy">\n        Economy\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Turks_and_Caicos_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Economy">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <p>\n       In 2009, GDP contributions were as follows:\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-quickstat1_67-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-quickstat1-67">\n         [64]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Hotels &amp; Restaurants 34.67%,\n       <a href="/wiki/Tax_haven" title="Tax haven">\n        Financial Services\n       </a>\n       13.12%, Construction 7.83%, Transport, Storage &amp; Communication 9.90%, and Real Estate, Renting &amp; Business Activities 9.56%.\n       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="margin-left:0.1em; white-space:nowrap;">\n        [\n        <i>\n         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Please_clarify" title="Wikipedia:Please clarify">\n          <span title="The text near this tag may need clarification or removal of jargon. (February 2009)">\n           clarification needed\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </i>\n        ]\n       </sup>\n       Most capital goods and food for domestic consumption are imported.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In 2010/2011, major sources of government revenue included Import Duties (43.31%), Stamp Duty on Land Transaction (8.82%), Work Permits and Residency Fees (10.03%) and Accommodation Tax (24.95%). The territory\'s gross domestic product as of late 2009 is approximately US$795 million (per capita $24,273).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-quickstat1_67-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-quickstat1-67">\n         [64]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The labour force totalled 27,595 workers in 2008. The labour force distribution in 2006 is as follows:\n      </p>\n      <table class="wikitable" style="text-align:center; border:1px;">\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n         Skill level\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         Percentage\n        </th>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         Unskilled/Manual\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         53%\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         Semi-skilled\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         12%\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         Skilled\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         20%\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         Professional\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         15%\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       The unemployment rate in 2008 was 8.3%. In 2007\xe2\x80\x932008, the territory took in revenues of $206.79 million against expenditures of $235.85 million. In 1995, the island received economic aid worth $5.7 million. The territory\'s currency is the United States dollar, with a few government fines (such as airport infractions) being payable in\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Pounds_sterling" title="Pounds sterling">\n        pounds sterling\n       </a>\n       . Most commemorative coin issues are denominated in crowns.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The primary agricultural products include limited amounts of maize,\n       <a href="/wiki/Bean" title="Bean">\n        beans\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Cassava" title="Cassava">\n        cassava\n       </a>\n       (\n       <a href="/wiki/Tapioca" title="Tapioca">\n        tapioca\n       </a>\n       ) and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Citrus_fruits" title="Citrus fruits">\n        citrus fruits\n       </a>\n       . Fish and conch are the only significant export, with some $169.2 million of\n       <a href="/wiki/Lobster" title="Lobster">\n        lobster\n       </a>\n       , dried and fresh\n       <a href="/wiki/Conch" title="Conch">\n        conch\n       </a>\n       , and conch shells exported in 2000, primarily to the United Kingdom and the United States. In recent years, however, the catch has been declining. The territory used to be an important trans-shipment point for South American narcotics destined for the United States, but due to the ongoing pressure of a combined American, Bahamian and Turks and Caicos effort this trade has been greatly reduced.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The islands import food and beverages, tobacco, clothing, manufacture and construction materials, primarily from the United States and the United Kingdom. Imports totalled $581 million in 2007.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The islands produce and consume about 5 GWh of electricity, per year, all of which comes from fossil fuels.\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Tourism">\n        Tourism\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Turks_and_Caicos_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Tourism">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       The United States was the leading source of tourists in 1996, accounting for more than half of the 87,000 visitors; another major source of tourists is Canada. Tourist arrivals had risen to 264,887 in 2007 and to 351,498 by 2009. In 2010, a total of 245 cruise ships arrived at the Grand Turk Cruise Terminal, carrying a total of 617,863 visitors.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-68">\n        <a href="#cite_note-68">\n         [65]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Turks_and_Caicos_Islands_sunset.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1920" data-file-width="2560" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5f/Turks_and_Caicos_Islands_sunset.jpg/220px-Turks_and_Caicos_Islands_sunset.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5f/Turks_and_Caicos_Islands_sunset.jpg/330px-Turks_and_Caicos_Islands_sunset.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5f/Turks_and_Caicos_Islands_sunset.jpg/440px-Turks_and_Caicos_Islands_sunset.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Turks_and_Caicos_Islands_sunset.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         A Turks and Caicos sunset\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Grand_Turk_beach.JPG">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1536" data-file-width="2048" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8c/Grand_Turk_beach.JPG/220px-Grand_Turk_beach.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8c/Grand_Turk_beach.JPG/330px-Grand_Turk_beach.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8c/Grand_Turk_beach.JPG/440px-Grand_Turk_beach.JPG 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Grand_Turk_beach.JPG" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         View of the southwestern beach at\n         <a href="/wiki/Grand_Turk_Island" title="Grand Turk Island">\n          Grand Turk Island\n         </a>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The government is pursuing a two-pronged strategy to increase tourism. Upscale resorts are aimed at the wealthy, while a large new\n       <a href="/wiki/Cruise_ship" title="Cruise ship">\n        cruise ship\n       </a>\n       port and recreation centre has been built for the masses visiting Grand Turk. Turks and Caicos Islands has one of the longest coral reefs in the world\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-69">\n        <a href="#cite_note-69">\n         [66]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and the world\'s only\n       <a href="/wiki/Conch" title="Conch">\n        conch\n       </a>\n       farm.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-70">\n        <a href="#cite_note-70">\n         [67]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The French vacation village company of\n       <a href="/wiki/Club_Med" title="Club Med">\n        Club Mediterannee\n       </a>\n       (Club Med) has an all-inclusive adult resort called \'Turkoise\' on one of the main islands.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Several Hollywood stars have built homes in the Turks and Caicos, including\n       <a href="/wiki/Dick_Clark" title="Dick Clark">\n        Dick Clark\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Bruce_Willis" title="Bruce Willis">\n        Bruce Willis\n       </a>\n       .\n       <a href="/wiki/Ben_Affleck" title="Ben Affleck">\n        Ben Affleck\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Jennifer_Garner" title="Jennifer Garner">\n        Jennifer Garner\n       </a>\n       married on\n       <a href="/wiki/Parrot_Cay" title="Parrot Cay">\n        Parrot Cay\n       </a>\n       in 2005. Actress\n       <a href="/wiki/Eva_Longoria" title="Eva Longoria">\n        Eva Longoria\n       </a>\n       and her ex-husband\n       <a href="/wiki/Tony_Parker" title="Tony Parker">\n        Tony Parker\n       </a>\n       went to the islands for their honeymoon in July 2007 and\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/High_School_Musical" title="High School Musical">\n         High School Musical\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       actors\n       <a href="/wiki/Zac_Efron" title="Zac Efron">\n        Zac Efron\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Vanessa_Hudgens" title="Vanessa Hudgens">\n        Vanessa Hudgens\n       </a>\n       went for a vacation there. In 2013 Hollywood writer/director\n       <a href="/wiki/Rob_Margolies" title="Rob Margolies">\n        Rob Margolies\n       </a>\n       and actress\n       <a href="/wiki/Kristen_Ruhlin" title="Kristen Ruhlin">\n        Kristen Ruhlin\n       </a>\n       vacationed here. Musician\n       <a href="/wiki/Nile_Rodgers" title="Nile Rodgers">\n        Nile Rodgers\n       </a>\n       has a vacation home on the island.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       To boost tourism during the Caribbean low season of late summer, since 2003 the Turks and Caicos Tourist Board have organised and hosted an annual series of concerts during this season called the Turks &amp; Caicos Music and Cultural Festival.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-71">\n        <a href="#cite_note-71">\n         [68]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Held in a temporary bandshell at The Turtle Cove Marina in\n       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=The_Bight&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="The Bight (page does not exist)">\n        The Bight\n       </a>\n       on\n       <a href="/wiki/Providenciales" title="Providenciales">\n        Providenciales\n       </a>\n       , this festival lasts about a week and has featured several notable international recording artists, such as\n       <a href="/wiki/Lionel_Richie" title="Lionel Richie">\n        Lionel Richie\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/LL_Cool_J" title="LL Cool J">\n        LL Cool J\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Anita_Baker" title="Anita Baker">\n        Anita Baker\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Billy_Ocean" title="Billy Ocean">\n        Billy Ocean\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Alicia_Keys" title="Alicia Keys">\n        Alicia Keys\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/John_Legend" title="John Legend">\n        John Legend\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Kenny_Rogers" title="Kenny Rogers">\n        Kenny Rogers\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Michael_Bolton" title="Michael Bolton">\n        Michael Bolton\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Ludacris" title="Ludacris">\n        Ludacris\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Chaka_Khan" title="Chaka Khan">\n        Chaka Khan\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Boyz_II_Men" title="Boyz II Men">\n        Boyz II Men\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-musicfestival.tc_72-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-musicfestival.tc-72">\n         [69]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       More than 10,000 people attend annually.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-musicfestival.tc_72-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-musicfestival.tc-72">\n         [69]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Resorts">\n        Resorts\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Turks_and_Caicos_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Resorts">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Grace_Bay_Resorts&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Grace Bay Resorts (page does not exist)">\n         Grace Bay Club\n        </a>\n        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-73">\n         <a href="#cite_note-73">\n          [70]\n         </a>\n        </sup>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=The_Somerset_on_Grace_Bay&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="The Somerset on Grace Bay (page does not exist)">\n         The Somerset on Grace Bay\n        </a>\n        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-74">\n         <a href="#cite_note-74">\n          [71]\n         </a>\n        </sup>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Beaches_Resorts" title="Beaches Resorts">\n         Beaches Resorts\n        </a>\n        \xe2\x80\x93 Turks &amp; Caicos\n        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-75">\n         <a href="#cite_note-75">\n          [72]\n         </a>\n        </sup>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        Seven Stars Resort\n        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-76">\n         <a </a>\n        </sup>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Biodiversity">\n        Biodiversity\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Turks_and_Caicos_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Biodiversity">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:French_Angelfish.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2361" data-file-width="3148" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2d/French_Angelfish.jpg/220px-French_Angelfish.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2d/French_Angelfish.jpg/330px-French_Angelfish.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2d/French_Angelfish.jpg/440px-French_Angelfish.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:French_Angelfish.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         A\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/French_Angelfish" title="French Angelfish">\n          French Angelfish\n         </a>\n         in Princess Alexandra Land and Sea National Park, Providenciales\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Blue_Tang_and_Squirrelfish.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3000" data-file-width="4000" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a1/Blue_Tang_and_Squirrelfish.jpg/220px-Blue_Tang_and_Squirrelfish.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a1/Blue_Tang_and_Squirrelfish.jpg/330px-Blue_Tang_and_Squirrelfish.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a1/Blue_Tang_and_Squirrelfish.jpg/440px-Blue_Tang_and_Squirrelfish.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Blue_Tang_and_Squirrelfish.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         A\n         <a href="/wiki/Acanthurus_coeruleus" title="Acanthurus coeruleus">\n          Blue Tang\n         </a>\n         and a\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Squirrelfish" title="Squirrelfish">\n          Squirrelfish\n         </a>\n         in Princess Alexandra Land and Sea National Park, Providenciales\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Whale-off-south-caicos.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="484" data-file-width="860" height="124" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Whale-off-south-caicos.jpg/220px-Whale-off-south-caicos.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Whale-off-south-caicos.jpg/330px-Whale-off-south-caicos.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Whale-off-south-caicos.jpg/440px-Whale-off-south-caicos.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Whale-off-south-caicos.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         <a href="/wiki/Humpback_whale" title="Humpback whale">\n          Humpback whale\n         </a>\n         breaching off\n         <a href="/wiki/South_Caicos" title="South Caicos">\n          South Caicos\n         </a>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The Turks and Caicos Islands are a\n       <a href="/wiki/Biodiversity_hotspot" title="Biodiversity hotspot">\n        biodiversity hotspot\n       </a>\n       . The islands have many endemic species and others of international importance, due to the conditions created by the oldest established salt-pan development in the Caribbean. The variety of species includes a number of endemic species of lizards, snakes, insects and plants, and marine organisms; in addition to being an important breeding area for seabirds.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-79">\n        <a href="#cite_note-79">\n         [76]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The UK and Turks and Caicos Islands Governments have joint responsibility for the conservation and preservation to meet obligations under international environmental conventions.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-80">\n        <a href="#cite_note-80">\n         [77]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Due to this significance, the islands are on the United Kingdom\'s tentative list for future\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/UNESCO_World_Heritage_Site" title="UNESCO World Heritage Site">\n        UNESCO World Heritage Sites\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-81">\n        <a href="#cite_note-81">\n         [78]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Transportation">\n        Transportation\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Turks_and_Caicos_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Transportation">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <p>\n       <a href="/wiki/Providenciales_International_Airport" title="Providenciales International Airport">\n        Providenciales International Airport\n       </a>\n       is the main entry point for the Turks and Caicos Islands. Altogether, there are seven airports, located on each of the inhabited islands. Five have paved runways (three of which are approximately 2,000\xc2\xa0m (6,600\xc2\xa0ft) long and one is approximately 1,000\xc2\xa0m (3,300\xc2\xa0ft) long), and the remaining two have unpaved runways (one of which is approximately 1,000\xc2\xa0m (3,300\xc2\xa0ft)s long and the other is significantly shorter).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-airporttech_82-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-airporttech-82">\n         [79]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The islands have 121 kilometres (75 miles) of highway, 24\xc2\xa0km (15\xc2\xa0mi) paved and 97\xc2\xa0km (60\xc2\xa0mi) unpaved. Like the\n       <a href="/wiki/United_States_Virgin_Islands" title="United States Virgin Islands">\n        United States Virgin Islands\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/British_Virgin_Islands" title="British Virgin Islands">\n        British Virgin Islands\n       </a>\n       , the Turks and Caicos Islands\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Drive_on_the_left" title="Drive on the left">\n        drive on the left\n       </a>\n       , but use left-hand-drive vehicles that are imported from the United States.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-suntci_83-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-suntci-83">\n         [80]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The territory\'s main international ports and harbours are on\n       <a href="/wiki/Grand_Turk_Island" title="Grand Turk Island">\n        Grand Turk\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Providenciales" title="Providenciales">\n        Providenciales\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-frommers_84-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-frommers-84">\n         [81]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The islands have no significant railways. In the early twentieth century\n       <a href="/wiki/East_Caicos" title="East Caicos">\n        East Caicos\n       </a>\n       operated a horse-drawn railway to transport\n       <a href="/wiki/Sisal" title="Sisal">\n        Sisal\n       </a>\n       from the plantation to the port. The 14-kilometre (8.7-mile) route was removed after sisal trading ceased.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-85">\n        <a href="#cite_note-85">\n         [82]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Postal_system">\n        Postal system\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Turks_and_Caicos_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: Postal system">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <p>\n       There is no postal delivery in the Turks and Caicos; mail is picked up at one of four post offices on each of the major islands.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-86">\n        <a href="#cite_note-86">\n         [83]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Mail is transported three or seven times a week, depending on the destination.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-87">\n        <a href="#cite_note-87">\n         [84]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The Post Office is part of the territory\'s government and reports to the Minister of Government Support Services.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-88">\n        <a href="#cite_note-88">\n         [85]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Media">\n        Media\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Turks_and_Caicos_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Media">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <p>\n       Mobile phone service is provided by\n       <a href="/wiki/Cable_%26_Wireless_Communications" title="Cable &amp; Wireless Communications">\n        Cable &amp; Wireless Communications\n       </a>\n       , through its\n       <a href="/wiki/Flow_(brand)" title="Flow (brand)">\n        Flow\n       </a>\n       brand, using\n       <a href="/wiki/GSM" title="GSM">\n        GSM\n       </a>\n       850 and\n       <a href="/wiki/Digital_AMPS" title="Digital AMPS">\n        TDMA\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Digicel" title="Digicel">\n        Digicel\n       </a>\n       , using GSM 900 and 1900 and Islandcom Wireless, using 3G 850. Cable &amp; Wireless provides CDMA mobile phone service in Providenciales and Grand Turk. The system is connected to the mainland by two submarine cables and an\n       <a href="/wiki/Intelsat" title="Intelsat">\n        Intelsat\n       </a>\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Earth_station" title="Earth station">\n        earth station\n       </a>\n       . There were three\n       <a href="/wiki/AM_broadcasting" title="AM broadcasting">\n        AM radio\n       </a>\n       stations (one inactive) and six\n       <a href="/wiki/FM_broadcasting" title="FM broadcasting">\n        FM\n       </a>\n       stations (no shortwave) in 1998. The most popular station is Power 92.5 FM which plays Top 100 hits. Over 8000 radio receivers are owned across the territory.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       West Indies Video (WIV) has been the sole cable television provider for the Turks and Caicos Islands for over two decades and WIV4 (a subsidiary of WIV) has been the only broadcast station in the islands for over 15 years; broadcasts from the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bahamas" title="Bahamas">\n        Bahamas\n       </a>\n       can also be received. The territory has two\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Internet_service_providers" title="Internet service providers">\n        internet service providers\n       </a>\n       and its\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Country_codes" title="Country codes">\n        country code\n       </a>\n       top level domain (ccTLD) is ".tc".\n       <a href="/wiki/Amateur_radio" title="Amateur radio">\n        Amateur radio\n       </a>\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Callsign" title="Callsign">\n        callsigns\n       </a>\n       begin with "VP5" and visiting operators frequently work from the islands.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       WIV introduced Channel 4 News in 2002 broadcasting local news and infotainment programs across the country. Channel 4 was re-launched as WIV4 in November 2007.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Since 2013 4NEWS has become the Islands first HD Cable News service with Television Studios in Grace Bay, Providenciales. DigicelPlay is the local cable provider.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Turks and Caicos\'s newspapers include the\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/Turks_and_Caicos_Weekly_News" title="Turks and Caicos Weekly News">\n         Turks and Caicos Weekly News\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       , the\n       <i>\n        <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Turks_and_Caicos_SUN&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Turks and Caicos SUN (page does not exist)">\n         Turks and Caicos SUN\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-89">\n        <a href="#cite_note-89">\n         [86]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and the\n       <i>\n        Turks and Caicos Free Press\n       </i>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-90">\n        <a href="#cite_note-90">\n         [87]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       All three publications are weekly. The\n       <i>\n        Weekly News\n       </i>\n       and the\n       <i>\n        Sun\n       </i>\n       both have supplement magazines. Other local magazines\n       <i>\n        Times of the Islands\n       </i>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-91">\n        <a href="#cite_note-91">\n         [88]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <i>\n        s3 Magazine\n       </i>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-92">\n        <a href="#cite_note-92">\n         [89]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <i>\n        Real Life Magazine\n       </i>\n       ,\n       <i>\n        Baller Magazine\n       </i>\n       , and\n       <i>\n        Unleashed Magazine\n       </i>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Spaceflight">\n        Spaceflight\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Turks_and_Caicos_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: Spaceflight">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <p>\n       From 1950 to 1981, the United States had a missile\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tracking_station" title="Tracking station">\n        tracking station\n       </a>\n       on Grand Turk. In the early days of the American space program,\n       <a href="/wiki/NASA" title="NASA">\n        NASA\n       </a>\n       used it. After his three earth orbits in 1962, American\n       <a href="/wiki/Astronaut" title="Astronaut">\n        astronaut\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/John_Glenn" title="John Glenn">\n        John Glenn\n       </a>\n       successfully landed in the nearby ocean and was brought back ashore to Grand Turk island.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-93">\n        <a href="#cite_note-93">\n         [90]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-94">\n        <a href="#cite_note-94">\n         [91]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Sports">\n        Sports\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Turks_and_Caicos_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: Sports">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <p>\n       <a href="/wiki/Cricket" title="Cricket">\n        Cricket\n       </a>\n       is the islands\'\n       <a href="/wiki/National_sport" title="National sport">\n        national sport\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ICC_95-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ICC-95">\n         [92]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Turks_and_Caicos_Islands_cricket_team" title="Turks and Caicos Islands cricket team">\n        national team\n       </a>\n       takes part in regional tournaments in the\n       <a href="/wiki/ICC_Americas_Championship" title="ICC Americas Championship">\n        ICC Americas Championship\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-96">\n        <a href="#cite_note-96">\n         [93]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       as well as having played one\n       <a href="/wiki/Twenty20" title="Twenty20">\n        Twenty20\n       </a>\n       match as part of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Stanford_20/20#2008_tournament" title="Stanford 20/20">\n        2008 Standford 20/20\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-97">\n        <a href="#cite_note-97">\n         [94]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Two domestic leagues exist, one on Grand Turk with three teams and another on Providenciales.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ICC_95-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ICC-95">\n         [92]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       As of 4 July 2012,\n       <a href="/wiki/Turks_and_Caicos_Islands_national_football_team" title="Turks and Caicos Islands national football team">\n        Turks and Caicos Islands\' football team\n       </a>\n       shared the position of the lowest ranking national men\'s football team in the world at the rank of 207th.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-98">\n        <a href="#cite_note-98">\n         [95]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Because the territory is not recognized by the\n       <a href="/wiki/International_Olympic_Committee" title="International Olympic Committee">\n        International Olympic Committee\n       </a>\n       , Turks and Caicos Islanders compete for\n       <a href="/wiki/Great_Britain" title="Great Britain">\n        Great Britain\n       </a>\n       at the\n       <a href="/wiki/Olympic_Games" title="Olympic Games">\n        Olympic Games\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-99">\n        <a href="#cite_note-99">\n         [96]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Notable_people">\n        Notable people\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Turks_and_Caicos_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=39" title="Edit section: Notable people">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="sport">\n        sport\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Turks_and_Caicos_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=40" title="Edit section: sport">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Christopher_Bryan" title="Christopher Bryan">\n         Christopher Bryan\n        </a>\n        (born 1960 in the Turks and Caicos Islands) is a former association football player. In 2006 he became the President of the\n        <a href="/wiki/Turks_and_Caicos_Islands_Football_Association" title="Turks and Caicos Islands Football Association">\n         Turks and Caicos Islands Football Association\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Errion_Charles" title="Errion Charles">\n         Errion Charles\n        </a>\n        (born 1965 in Saint Vincent) is a sportsman from the Turks and Caicos Islands who has represented his nation at both association football and cricket\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Gregory_Watts" title="Gregory Watts">\n         Gregory Watts\n        </a>\n        (born 1967 in the Turks and Caicos Islands) is a former footballer, he played as a defender\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Gavin_Glinton" title="Gavin Glinton">\n         Gavin Glinton\n        </a>\n        (born 1979 in Grand Turk) is a footballer who last played for\n        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Nam_Dinh_FC" title="Nam Dinh FC">\n         Nam Dinh FC\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Trevor_Ariza" title="Trevor Ariza">\n         Trevor Ariza\n        </a>\n        (born 1985 in Miami) is an American professional basketball player for the Houston Rockets. He is of Turks &amp; Caicos Islands and Dominican descent through his parents, Lolita Ariza and Trevor Saunders of Grand Turk\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Delano_Williams" title="Delano Williams">\n         Delano Williams\n        </a>\n        (born 1993 in Grand Turk) is a British sprinter. He trains with the\n        <a href="/wiki/Racers_Track_Club" title="Racers Track Club">\n         Racers Track Club\n        </a>\n        in Jamaica\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="politics_2">\n        politics\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Turks_and_Caicos_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=41" title="Edit section: politics">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Nathaniel_Francis" title="Nathaniel Francis">\n         Nathaniel Francis\n        </a>\n        (1912 \xe2\x80\x93 2004 both in the Turks and Caicos Islands) was a politician who served as the island territory\'s acting Chief Minister from 28 March 1985 until 25 July 1986, when he was forced to resign after charges of corruption and patronage were leveled against him\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Clement_Howell" title="Clement Howell">\n         Clement Howell\n        </a>\n        (1935 in Blue Hills, Providenciales - 1987 near Nassau, Bahamas) was a politician who served on a four-member interim Advisory Council beginning in July 1986\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Norman_Saunders_(politician)" title="Norman Saunders (politician)">\n         Norman B. Saunders\n        </a>\n        (born 1943 in the Turks and Caicos Islands) is a former politician who served as the island territory\'s Chief Minister until March 1985, when he was arrested in Miami. In July 1985 he was sentenced to eight years in prison on conspiracy charges related to drug smuggling.\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/James_Alexander_George_Smith_McCartney" title="James Alexander George Smith McCartney">\n         James Alexander George Smith McCartney\n        </a>\n        (1945 in Grand Turk \xe2\x80\x93 1980 in New Jersey) also known as "Jags" McCartney was a politician who served as the island territory\'s first Chief Minister from August 1976 until 9 May 1980, when he died in a plane crash over New Jersey.\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Washington_Misick" title="Washington Misick">\n         Washington Misick\n        </a>\n        (born 1950 in the Turks and Caicos Islands) is a politician who served as the island territory\'s Chief Minister from April 1991 to 31 January 1995.\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Ariel_Misick" title="Ariel Misick">\n         Ariel Misick\n        </a>\n        (born 1951) is a former minister of development and commerce. He served on a four-member interim Advisory Council from July 1986 to 3 March 1988\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Oswald_Skippings" title="Oswald Skippings">\n         Oswald Skippings\n        </a>\n        (born 1953 in the Turks and Caicos Islands) is a politician who served as the island territory\'s Chief Minister from 19 June 1980 to November 1980 and again from 3 March 1988 to April 1991.\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Michael_Misick" title="Michael Misick">\n         Michael Misick\n        </a>\n        (born 1966 in Bottle Creek, North Caicos) is the former chief minister from 15 August 2003 to 9 August 2006 and was the first Premier from 9 August 2006 to 23 March 2009. He is on trial for conspiracy to receive bribes, conspiracy to defraud the government and money laundering.\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="See_also">\n ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div aria-label="Portals" class="noprint portal plainlist tright" role="navigation" style="margin:0.5em 0 0.5em 1em;border:solid #aaa 1px">\n Islands">\n         Outline of the Turks and Caicos Islands\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Index_of_Turks_and_Caicos_Islands-related_articles" title="Index of Turks and Caicos Islands-related articles">\n         Index of Turks and Caicos Islands-related articles\n        </a>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Notes">\n        Notes\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div class="reflist columns references-column-width" style="-moz-column-width: 30em; -webkit-column-width: 30em; column-width: 30em; list-style-type: </li>\n        <li id="cite_note-area-8">\n         <span class="mw-cite-backlink">\n          ^\n          <a href="#cite_ref-area_8-0">\n           <sup>\n            <i>\n             <b>\n              a\n             </b>\n            </i>\n           </sup>\n          </a>\n          <a href="#cite_ref-area_8-1">\n           <sup>\n            <i>\n             <b>\n              b\n             </b>\n            </i>\n           </sup>\n          </a>\n         </span>\n         <span class="reference-text">\n          Different sources give different figures for the Islands\' area.\n          <i>\n           The CIA World Factbook\n          </i>\n          gives 430\xc2\xa0km\n          <sup>\n           2\n          </sup>\n          ,\n          <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-cia_4-0">\n           <a href="#cite_note-cia-4">\n            [3]\n           </a>\n          </sup>\n          the European Union says 417 km\n          <sup>\n           2\n          </sup>\n          ,\n          <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-5">\n           <a href="#cite_note-5">\n            [4]\n           </a>\n          </sup>\n          and the Encyclop\xc3\xa6dia Britannica says "Area at high tide, 238 square miles (616 square km); at low tide, 366 square miles (948 square km)".\n          <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-6">\n           <a href="#cite_note-6">\n            [5]\n           </a>\n          </sup>\n          A report by the Turks and Caicos Islands Department of Economic Planning and Statistics gives the same numbers as the Encyclop\xc3\xa6dia Britannica though its definitions are less clear.\n          <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-7">\n           <a href="#cite_note-7">\n            [6]\n           </a>\n          </sup>\n         </span>\n        </li>\n        <li id="cite_note-61">\n         <span class="mw-cite-backlink">\n          <b>\n           <a href="#cite_ref-61">\n            ^\n           </a>\n          </b>\n         </span>\n         <span class="reference-text">\n          The Islands area and population data retrieved from the 2012 census\n         </span>\n        </li>\n                 unrecognised\n                     </a>\n                     state until the 1979\n                     <a href="/wiki/Lancaster_House_Agreement" title="Lancaster House Agreement">\n                      Lancaster House Agreement\n                     </a>\n                     . After recognised independence in 1980, Zimbabwe was a member of the Commonwealth until it withdrew in 2003.\n                    </li>\n                   </ul>\n                  </div>\n were previously dependencies of Saint Helena.\n                    </li>\n                    <li>\n                     15.\xc2\xa0Both claimed in 1908; territories formed in 1962 (British Antarctic
